 126: 
 127: def wait_for_openclaw_result(
 128:     api_base: str,
 129:     task_id: str,
 130:     *,
 131:     api_token: str = "",
 132:     timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
 133:     poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
 134:     request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
 135:     session: Any = None,
 136: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 137:     deadline = time.time() + max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds))
 138:     while True:
 139:         payload = fetch_openclaw_result(
 140:             api_base=api_base,
 141:             task_id=task_id,
 142:             api_token=api_token,
 143:             timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
 144:             session=session,
 145:         )
 146:         result = payload.get("openclaw_result") if isinstance(payload.get("openclaw_result"), dict) else {}
 147:         status = str(result.get("status") or "").strip().lower()
 148:         if status in {"completed", "failed", "cancelled"}:
 149:             return payload
 150:         if time.time() >= deadline:
 151:             raise TimeoutError(f"wait openclaw result timed out: task_id={task_id} status={status or 'unknown'}")
 152:         time.sleep(max(0.2, float(poll_interval_seconds)))
 153: 
 154: 
 155: def run_openclaw_video_task(
 156:     api_base: str,
 157:     video_path: str | Path,
 158:     *,
 159:     api_token: str = "",
 160:     task_id: str = "",
 161:     source: str = "openclaw_client",
 162:     stage5_model_name: str = "",
 163:     extra_form: Mapping[str, Any] | None = None,
 164:     wait: bool = True,
 165:     submit_timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,
 166:     wait_timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
 167:     poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
 168:     request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
 169:     session: Any = None,
 170: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 171:     submitted = submit_openclaw_video_task(
 172:         api_base=api_base,
 173:         video_path=video_path,
 174:         api_token=api_token,
 175:         task_id=task_id,
 176:         source=source,
 177:         stage5_model_name=stage5_model_name,
 178:         extra_form=extra_form,
 179:         timeout_seconds=submit_timeout_seconds,
 180:         session=session,
 181:     )
 182:     output = {"submit": submitted}
 183:     if not wait:
 184:         return output
 185: 
 186:     resolved_task_id = str(submitted.get("task_id") or "").strip()
 187:     if not resolved_task_id:
 188:         raise RuntimeError("submit response missing task_id")
 189:     output["result"] = wait_for_openclaw_result(
 190:         api_base=api_base,
 191:         task_id=resolved_task_id,
 192:         api_token=api_token,
 193:         timeout_seconds=wait_timeout_seconds,
 194:         poll_interval_seconds=poll_interval_seconds,
 195:         request_timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
 196:         session=session,
 197:     )
 198:     return output

+# Video Pipeline Startup Implementation Plan
+
+> **For agentic workers:** REQUIRED SUB-SKILL: Use superpowers:subagent-driven-development (recommended) or superpowers:executing-plans to implement this plan task-by-task. Steps use checkbox (`- [ ]`) syntax for tracking.
+
+**Goal:** Restore the new `VideoPipeline` path as the real foundation for CloneCut, then cut worker/API/result contracts over without reintroducing old-architecture fallback.
+
+**Architecture:** Start from the narrowest unblocker first: recreate the `domain.video.stages` package so `domain.video.pipeline` and its tests can run at all. Then port the contract-critical stages and artifact/manfiest behavior that current API/client flows already depend on. Only after the pipeline contract is stable should worker execution and API/result envelopes switch to the new path.
+
+**Tech Stack:** Python, pytest, Flask API, worker queue/service, file-based stage artifacts/manifests
+

+

+- [ ] **Step 3: Add the minimum shared stage contract**
+
+Create `domain/video/stages/base.py` with one small result object that every stage returns.
+
+```python
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+from typing import Any
+
+
+@dataclass
+class StageResult:
+    success: bool
+    output_file: str | None = None
+    error_message: str | None = None
+    manifest_path: str | None = None
+    metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
+```
+
+Create `domain/video/stages/utils.py` with the first shared helpers only:
+
+```python
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from pathlib import Path
+
+
+def ensure_stage_dir(output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> Path:
+    stage_dir = Path(output_dir) / task_id / "_stages"
+    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
+    return stage_dir
+
+
+def probe_duration_seconds(_input_video: str) -> float:
+    return 0.0
+```
+
+- [ ] **Step 4: Add stage modules as minimal pass-through implementations**
+
+For each stage module, start with the smallest deterministic implementation that preserves file outputs and stage names instead of business accuracy. The job in this task is importability and pipeline shape, not algorithm parity.
+
+Pattern:
+
+```python
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from pathlib import Path
+
+from .base import StageResult
+from .utils import ensure_stage_dir
+
+
+def run_stage0_clean(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
+    ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
+    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=input_video)
+```
+
+Apply the same pattern to every `run_stageX_*` symbol used by `domain/video/pipeline.py`, with stage-specific output/manfiest files only where the current tests require them.
+
+- [ ] **Step 5: Re-export the new public entry**
+
+Replace `domain/video/__init__.py` empty exports with:
+
+```python
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from domain.video.config import VideoPipelineConfig
+from domain.video.pipeline import VideoPipeline
+
+__all__ = ["VideoPipeline", "VideoPipelineConfig"]
+```
+
+- [ ] **Step 6: Run the first unblock verification**

+

+### Task 3: Cut Worker and API/Client Contracts Over to the New Pipeline
+
+**Why third:** Only after the new pipeline produces stable artifacts should worker execution switch. This avoids debugging worker orchestration and stage parity at the same time.

+
+- [ ] **Step 1: Replace worker’s old internal pipeline path with `VideoPipeline`**
+
+Current reality to remove:
+
+- `_run_internal_video_pipeline()` shells into `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py`
+- warm runner failure still falls back to subprocess/copy mode
+
+Target:
+
+- Worker instantiates and runs `domain.video.VideoPipeline`
+- `executed_mode` reflects the new pipeline path
+- old fallback copy/subprocess remains visible only if explicitly retained as migration-only, not silent mainline behavior
+

+```powershell

+

+    ...

+## Startup Recommendation
+
+If only one engineer starts coding today, the safest order is:
+
+1. **Task 1 first**
+   - Lowest risk
+   - Fastest feedback
+   - Unlocks import/test collection immediately
+2. **Task 2 second**
+   - Stabilizes the artifact and manifest contracts the rest of the system already relies on
+   - Avoids mixing worker orchestration bugs with stage porting bugs
+3. **Task 3 third**
+   - Performs the risky cutover only after the new pipeline already behaves like a real producer
+
+## Self-Review
+
+- Spec coverage:
+  - Core pipeline unblock: covered by Task 1
+  - Contract-critical stage parity: covered by Task 2
+  - Worker/API/client cutover: covered by Task 3
+- Placeholder scan:
+  - No `TBD`, `TODO`, or “implement later” placeholders remain
+- Type consistency:
+  - Plan consistently uses `task_spec`, `progress_event`, `artifact_manifest`, `VideoPipeline`, and `StageResult`

Plan
计划已写入 [2026-03-28-video-pipeline-startup-plan.md](D:/clonecut/docs/superpowers/plans/2026-03-28-video-pipeline-startup-plan.md)。

最稳的 3 个启动代码任务是：
- 先恢复 domain/video/stages 骨架和 domain.video 公共导出，让 VideoPipeline 能导入、测试能开始执行。
- 再优先迁移契约敏感的 stages：stage4/5/6/6.5/7/8/9，先把字幕、封面、clip_text、manifest、artifacts 这些现有 API/客户端依赖的结果稳定下来，stage3_repair 只保留最小实现。
- 最后再切 apps/worker/service.py 和 apps/api/main.py，让 worker 真正调用 VideoPipeline，同时给 openclaw_result / render_manifest 加 schema_version，并守住客户端契约测试。

为什么这个顺序最稳
因为现在最大的风险不是 OpenClaw，而是新主链还没成为一个可运行、可产出稳定结果的生产者。先修骨架，再修结果契约，最后做 worker/API 切换，能把“阶段实现问题”和“编排接线问题”拆开排查，不会同时爆两层。
